Mental Fuel   (motivation source)
External Motivation Source
(Motivation that lead by fear, insecurity, 
materialism)

- fear 
    + mundane task
    + being average
    + risk of assimilate back into the system
    + last chance of improvement this young 
       with huge trajectory & momentum.
    + losing momentum that I build 
      continuously for 3 years.
 
- trauma (little left, have used it all)
- potential (some left, the older the lesser)
- ego/identity activate through environment
    + environment = friends + surrounding habitat

Internal Motivation Source 
- physical wellbeing
    + calisthenics
    + good food
- personal goals
    + be a good parent
    + make myself proud -> achieve true self-freedom
    + have a beautiful & smart wife/children
    + become a independent researcher/developer
    + achieve certified calisthenics skills (planche, front-level, maltese) 


 ^RiMBy0oa

Push myself -> do my best -> stress 
-> play game / mindless -> disappointed -> self-adjustment ^ILqTqElQ

Old self: 
- fixed high-expectation for thing (done everything in once) -> too stress -> do nothing. 
    + unrealistic
- fixed linear works (I must finished this before doing that)
    + lack dynamic/adaptation/flexibility
- low responsibility without supervisor
    + root cause: not accepting it will be hard, require doing a lot of thing, 
       want to have more fun without work <- downfall after playing videogame again. 
- impulsive behavior causes by stress
    + mindless content (short) -> fix by using "minimal YouTube homepage"
    + playing game to kill time & stress -> fix by realizing higher purpose and being Zen for a few days.
- Restrict myself from experience new things if I don't doing good at current thing. ^X7KGAd2y

repeat ^VEV8wnHx

Mental Drain   (De-Motivation)
- Negative Energy
    + Wasting Time
    + Messy Environment
    + Not taking responsibility

- Mundane Task
    + repetitive task / un-novelty task 
       even though it novel once
    

 ^7AnX1uhw

crave stimulant
to get back 
on track ^W3ZAPxDU

Game, Hangout, Sleep,
Wasting Time until self-adjustment hit. ^vHpAqRsU

Mental rabbit hole (action that I though could solve my problem but actually causes more problem)
- tomorrow I will do it (recite Deepthough.md)
- playing game first thing in the morning 
    + bc I think it would give me motivation to do                                
      other stuff instead of doing nothing. 
    -> false because doing nothing literally solve the  
       problem. Root cause come from overstimulation.
- short-burst of long gaming hours -> could be good at first but very easy to fall back into old gaming habit again.
 ^DZ7areK1

Improvement Cycle ^KelBwcmi

Solution (what I haven't try yet):
- Being Zen for more than 1-2 weeks. 
At threshold either 
doing nothing or study something, no playing in between, 
try to preserve mental energy 
<-> don't need to spend them all on calisthenics.  

- Allow myself to do everything I Interested 
  in when the deadline isn't close.
     + Boost Efficiency bc at least I do sth rather than playing.
     + More Motivated to do Stuff bc of deadline 
    -> this is "ADHD/Energy management, not procrastination"
    -> Same principle with Buy High, Sell Low I guess :))         
 ^TxSdM4uM

being Zen mean 
+ no overstimulation like video game, sexual stimulant.
+ no coffee in the morning & after 2PM.
+ no YouTube short or Recommendation (minimal YouTube only). ^Ga0UCz9X

Benefits
more control
active thinking
peace
quicker study recovery
better sleep quality
sharper mind
 ^DmpRDBJs

Downside
- require better stress management
- on early stage
    + lower stress capacity 
    + risk of calisthenics performance
      decline
    + slower recovery  bc I suddenly 
      cutout my stimulant source
    -> risk of overstress & back to old habit 
        again if surpass. 
 ^GJyWKrds

Overcome Boredom + Stress System ^TLjfF1Rp

Alternative Stimulant Source 
through 7 types of Rest
- cooking (creative rest)
- violin (creative + emotional rest)
- calisthenics (physical rest) -> increase stress + fatigue if too much though. 
- game/YouTube -> short break, sleep or running (mental rest )
- writing, music, talk to ppl (emotional rest)
- minimal YouTube, silent mode, reduce screen time (sensory rest)
- calisthenics, social event with friend, family time (social rest)
- doing research, reading book, self-talk (spiritual rest)  
- personal coding project (emotional + spiritual + mental rest)
- learning language (creative rest)

- POSITIVE THINKING (instead of assigning Negative emotion or consequence
in task 
-> think of what I would gain or help/benefit others if I could finish this)
-> Mental model to convert (task) negative into positive. ^xZjUIMb3

+ alcohol
+ sugar
+ vitamin C affect 
adhd medication ^zjVIzB0H
